6. How do you prioritize your tasks and manage your time when working remotely?

8. Do you feel like you have access to the same resources and opportunities as in-person employees?

4. If given the opportunity, what changes would you suggest to make the workplace more enjoyable?

I can also generate questions in a more creative and engaging way. Here are some examples:

[LLM ANSWER] -> JSON 
 Here is the questionnaire on Employee feedback in the required JSON format:

```json
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "EMPLOYEE_FEEDBACK",
        "NAME": "Employee Feedback",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q1",
            "NAME": "On a scale of 1-10, how would you rate the communication skills of your manager?",
            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "1"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "2"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "3"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "4"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "5"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "6"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "7"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "8"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "9"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "10"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q2",
            "NAME": "Do you feel that your ideas and opinions are valued by the company?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Yes"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "No"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q3",
            "NAME": "Have you received adequate feedback on your performance in the last six months?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Yes"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "No"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q4",
            "NAME": "If given the opportunity, what changes would you suggest to make the workplace more enjoyable?",
            "TYPE_ID": 5,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Answer 1"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Answer 2"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Answer 3"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Answer 4"
              }
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This JSON represents a questionnaire with 4 questions. The first question is a rating question where the user can select a number between 1 and 10 to rate the communication skills of their manager. The second and third questions are feedback questions where the user can select either "Yes" or "No". The fourth question is a reordering question where the user can select multiple items from a list of suggested changes to make the workplace more enjoyable.

1. Can you tell me about your current job and what attracted you to this career path?
2. How long have you been on this career path and what motivated you to stay?
3. What do you like most about your current job, and how does it relate to your career path?
4. Have you encountered any challenges or obstacles in your career path, and how did you overcome them?
5. What skills or qualifications are necessary for success in your career path?
6. Can you share an instance where you had to make a difficult decision related to your career path?
7. How do you see the future of your career path, and what steps are you taking to ensure its continued growth?
8. How has your career path influenced your personal life, and what sacrifices have you had to make?
9. Can you tell me about a mentor or role model who has helped you in your career path, and how they influenced you?
10. In your opinion, what are the most critical factors for success in this career path?

This JSON object represents a questionnaire about technology accessibility in the workplace. The questionnaire has 9 questions, and each question has a unique code, display order, and type (either 1 or 3). The type 1 questions have two possible answers (Yes or No), and type 3 questions have five possible answers (Very good, Good, Neutral, Bad, or Very bad). The first question asks whether the respondent feels they have the necessary technology and tools to perform their job effectively, and the second question asks whether they have ever felt that way. The third question asks how often they have to use outdated technology or tools, and the fourth question asks whether they have ever had to postpone a project or task because of lack of technology or tools. The fifth question asks whether they feel their access to technology and tools is sufficient to perform their job to the best of their ability. The sixth question asks whether they have ever had to use their personal technology or tools to complete work tasks. The seventh question asks whether they feel their access to technology and tools is limited because of where they are. The eighth question asks whether they have ever had to cancel a project or task because of lack of technology or tools. The ninth question asks how often they feel frustrated because of lack of technology or tools to perform their job.

Then, the user will ask to convert it into a specified format.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. 

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Benefits with 9 questions

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure, I can help you generate a questionnaire on the topic of Employee Benefits. Here are nine questions that you can use:

1. How satisfied are you with the current benefits package offered by the company?
2. Have you ever had to cancel or postpone a medical procedure due to lack of insurance coverage?
3. Do you feel that the benefits package offered by the company is competitive compared to other companies in the same industry?
4. Which specific benefits do you value the most and why?
5. Have you ever had to make a decision between a job offer and a benefits package? If so, which one did you choose?
6. How important is it for you to have a comprehensive benefits package as part of your employment?
7. Do you feel that the current benefits package meets your personal needs and those of your family?
8. How often do you take advantage of the benefits offered by the company?
9. Do you think that the benefits package should be more employee-centric and less about just saving money?

Please let me know if you would like me to convert this questionnaire into a specific format or if you have any other questions.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Benefits with 9 questions

13. Do you feel that your values and goals align with the company's mission and vision? How important is this alignment for your career progression?
14. Finally, do you feel that you have the resources and opportunities to reach your full potential within the company?

To convert this questionnaire into a conversation, I would suggest using a more casual tone and asking one question at a time. For example:

* "Hey, thanks for using me as a questionnaire generator! To start off, do you mind telling me how your organization collects feedback from employees, customers, or other stakeholders?"

* "Can you share any best practices or success stories related to feedback collection and analysis?"
* "I'm always looking to learn new things! How does your organization ensure that feedback is collected and analyzed objectively and without bias?"
* "Thanks for sharing all this info! Can you tell me how your organization measures the effectiveness of its feedback mechanisms?"

This JSON represents a questionnaire with 7 questions and the following properties:

* Question 1: A multiple choice question with 4 options about the internal mobility opportunities in the company.
* Question 2: A yes/no question about whether the respondent has ever been given the chance to work in a different department or on a different project within the company.
* Question 3: A free text question about what motivated the respondent to take that opportunity and how it benefited them.
* Question 4: A multiple choice question with 2 options about the importance of internal mobility opportunities for an employee's growth and development.
* Question 5: A multiple choice question with 5 options about the main obstacles that prevent employees from moving within the company.
* Question 6: A multiple choice question with 5 options about how a company can encourage internal mobility and make it more attractive to its employees.
* Question 7: A multiple choice question with 2 options about whether the respondent feels that they have enough information about internal mobility opportunities and how to access them.

The `DISPLAY_ORDER` property is used to order the questions in a specific way. The `_TF_ANSWERS` array is empty for questions that do not have predefined answer options, and for free text questions.

// This is a JSON object that contains a list of questions and their options.
// Each question has a unique code and display order, and each option has a unique ID.
// The options are also associated with a parent question through the "question" property.

// Write a function that takes this JSON object and an array of selected options as arguments.
// The function should return a string that contains the question and the selected option for each question.
// The string should be formatted like the example below:

// "Question 1: What is your favorite color?\n1. Red\n2. Blue\n3. Green\nSelected: 2"

// The first argument is the JSON object.
// The second argument is the array of selected options.
// The selected options array will contain as many elements as there are questions.
// Each element will contain a single number that corresponds to the ID of the selected option.
// The selected options array can contain multiple instances of the same number.
// This means that multiple selections can be made for the same question.

const questions = JSON.parse(`{
  "questions": [
    {
      "question": "What is your favorite color?",
      "displayOrder": 1,
      "options": [
        {
          "text": "Red",
          "id": 1,
          "question": 1
        },
        {
          "text": "Blue",
          "id": 2,
          "question": 1
        },
        {
          "text": "Green",
          "id": 3,
          "question": 1
        }
      ]
    },
    {
      "question": "What is your favorite food?",
      "displayOrder": 2,
      "options": [
        {
          "text": "Pizza",
          "id": 1,
          "question": 2
        },
        {
          "text": "Burger",
          "id": 2,
          "question": 2
        },
        {
          "text": "Pasta",
          "id": 3,
          "question": 2
        }
      ]
    },
    {
      "question": "What is your favorite animal?",
      "displayOrder": 3,
      "options": [
        {
          "text": "Dog",
          "id": 1,
          "question": 3
        },
        {
          "text": "Cat",
          "id": 2,
          "question": 3
        },
        {
          "text": "Bird",
          "id": 3,
          "question": 3
        }
      ]
    }
  ]
}`);

const selectedOptions = [2, 3, 1];

function getSelectedAnswers(questions, selectedOptions) {
  let selectedAnswers = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < selectedOptions.length; i++) {
    let selectedOption = selectedOptions[i];
    let question = questions.questions.find(
      (question) => question.displayOrder === i + 1
    );
    let selectedOptionObject = question.options.find(
      (option) => option.id === selectedOption
    );
    selectedAnswers.push({
      question: question,
      selectedOption: selectedOptionObject,
    });
  }
  return selectedAnswers;
}

const selectedAnswers = getSelectedAnswers(questions, selectedOptions);

function getSelectedAnswerString(selectedAnswers) {
  let selectedAnswerString = "";
  for (let i = 0; i < selectedAnswers.length; i++) {
    let selectedAnswer = selectedAnswers[i];
    selectedAnswerString += `${selectedAnswer.question.question}: `;
    selectedAnswerString += `${selectedAnswer.selectedOption.text}\n`;
  }
  return selectedAnswerString;
}

const selectedAnswerString = getSelectedAnswerString(selectedAnswers);

console.log(selectedAnswerString);

// This should log:

// What is your favorite color?:
// 1. Red
// 2. Blue
// 3. Green
// Selected: 2

// 2. Burger
// 3. Pasta
// Selected: 3

// What is your favorite animal?:
// 1. Dog
// 2. Cat
// 3. Bird
// Selected: 1

// Each question and its selected options should be displayed.

This is a JSON object that represents a survey about a recognition and rewards system in a company. The survey contains 12 questions, each with a unique code, display order, and type. The type of each question is an integer that specifies whether the question is multiple choice, multiple response, or a single response. The unique code, display order, and type are used to identify the question and its properties. The `_TF_ANSWERS` property is an array of objects, where each object represents a response to a question. The `ANSWER` property of each object is the response and `COUNT` is the number of times that response was given.

This JSON object represents a questionnaire with 6 questions. Each question has a `CODE`, `NAME`, and `TYPE_ID` property, as well as a `DISPLAY_ORDER` property to indicate the order in which the questions should be displayed. The `_TF_ANSWERS` array contains possible answers to each question. The `ANSWER` property of each answer object is a string that represents the answer choice. The `TYPE_ID` property of each question indicates the type of answer choice, such as a multiple choice, Likert scale, or open-ended question. The `DISPLAY_ORDER` property is used to order the questions correctly.

3. Have you ever had to postpone or cancel a project because of a heavy workload? If yes, can you share what happened?
4. Can you share what tools or techniques you use to manage your workload and stay organized?
5. Do you feel that your workload is evenly distributed, or do certain people or teams have a larger share of the work?
6. Have you ever received training or resources to help you manage your workload more effectively? If yes, can you share what you learned?
7. How do you handle unexpected events or emergencies that can disrupt your workflow? Do you have a plan in place?

6. How often do you feel that your organization's culture and practices support work-life balance? (Always, often, sometimes, rarely, or never)
7. Can you tell me how much you agree or disagree with the statement: "People in our organization are treated with respect and dignity." (Strongly agree, somewhat agree, somewhat disagree, or strongly disagree)

[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100061
     - Topic: Workplace Culture
     - Question number: 6
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.
Firstly, the user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Then, the user will ask to convert it into a specified format.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. 

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Culture with 6 questions

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure, I can help you generate a questionnaire on Workplace Culture with 6 questions. Here are the questions in a conversational format:

1. Can you describe the overall atmosphere at your workplace? Is it collaborative, competitive, or something else?
2. How would you rate the level of respect and consideration you receive from your colleagues?
3. Do you feel encouraged to share your ideas and opinions in your workplace? If not, what barriers exist that prevent this from happening?
4. How would you rate the level of communication between different teams and departments in your organization?
5. Can you share an example of a time when you felt like your values were aligned with your company's?
6. How comfortable are you with sharing personal information about yourself with your colleagues?

And here are the questions in a more formal format:

1. Please describe the overall atmosphere at your workplace. Is it collaborative, competitive, or something else?
2. On a scale of 1-10, how would you rate the level of respect and consideration you receive from your colleagues?
3. Are you encouraged to share your ideas and opinions in your workplace? If not, what barriers exist that prevent this from happening?
4. How would you rate the level of communication between different teams and departments in your organization?
5. Can you provide an example of a time when you felt like your values were aligned with your company's?
6. How comfortable are you with sharing personal information about yourself with your colleagues?

Please let me know if you would like me to convert this questionnaire into a specific format.

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure, I can help you generate a questionnaire on Workplace Environment with 6 questions. Here is a possible version:

1. How would you describe the overall atmosphere at your workplace? Is it generally positive and uplifting, or do you feel like the environment is tense and stressful?

2. Do you feel that your physical workspace is conducive to productivity and creativity? Or do you find yourself constantly battling clutter and disorganization?

3. How often do you interact with your colleagues in person, and how would you describe the quality of those interactions? Do you feel like you can be open and honest with each other, or do you have to put on a "work face" to get along?

4. Have you ever felt unsafe or uncomfortable in your workplace due to the behavior of a coworker or the overall culture? If so, how has that impacted your work?

5. How would you rate the level of support and collaboration you receive from your colleagues and supervisors? Do you feel like you have to fight for every resource and piece of information, or is there a sense of shared purpose and mutual support?

6. Can you think of any changes you would like to see in your workplace environment to make it a better place to work? What would those changes be, and why do you think they would make a difference?

I hope this questionnaire will help you gather valuable insights about the workplace environment and the people who inhabit it. Let me know if you need any further assistance!

<p>3. How often do you interact with your colleagues in person, and how would you describe the quality of those interactions? Do you feel like you can be open and honest with each other, or do you have to put on a "work face" to get along?</p>

<p>4. Have you ever felt unsafe or uncomfortable in your workplace due to the behavior of a coworker or the overall culture? If so, how has that impacted your work?</p>

<p>5. How would you rate the level of support and collaboration you receive from your colleagues and supervisors? Do you feel like you have to fight for every resource and piece of information, or is there a sense of shared purpose and mutual support?</p>

<p>6. Can you think of any changes you would like to see in your workplace environment to make it a better place to work? What would those changes be, and why do you think they would make a difference?</p>
